div=int(input())
cant=int(input())
a=input().split(' ')
b=input().split(' ')
C=[]
A=[int(x) for x in a]
B=[int(q) for q in b]
for i in range (0,cant,1):
    c=A[i]*B[i]
    C.append(c)
Suma=sum(C)
Calculo=Suma/div
print (round(Calculo,1))

ardelgado:Problem1695:Runtime Error
div=int(input())
cant=int(input())
a=input().split(' ')
b=input().split(' ')
C=[]
for t in range (len(a)):
    a[t]=int(a[t])
for q in range (len(b)):
    b[q]=int(b[q])
for i in range (0,cant,1):
    c=a[i]*b[i]
    C.append(c)
Suma=sum(C)
Calculo=Suma/div
print (round(Calculo,1))

        n,k = map(int,input().split())
        contador = 1
        s = 0
        i = 0
        if i<=n<=100:
            x = True
        if i<=k<=100:
            y = True
        while x and y:
            s = s + (i+k)/(2+i+k)
            i = i + 1
            if contador > n:
                x = False
            contador = contador + 1
        print(int(s))
except EOFError:
    pass

#Evaluando...

import math

#Entrada
while True:
    try:
        n, k = map(int, input().split())
        while(1 > n > 100 and 1 > k > 100):
            n, k = map(int, input().split())
        #Proceso
        #suma
        suma = 0
        for i in range(0, n, 1):
            suma = suma + (i+k)/(2+i+k)
        suma = math.ceil(suma)
        
        print(suma)
    except EOFError:
        break

#Entrada
N = int(input())

#Proceso
for i in range(1, N+1, 1):
    a = -1
    b = 1
    c = 0
    n = int(input())
    while(n > 40 or n < 1):
        n = int(input())
        
    s = 0
    for j in range(1, n+1, 1):
        d = a + b + c
        a = b
        b = c
        c = d
        s = s + c
    #Salida
    print(s)

#Entrada

n, x = map(int, input().split())

    n, x = map(int, input().split())
    
#Valores
num = 2; d=2; flag = 1;#(Verdad) #n° Primos
a = 1;b = 0 #fibonacci
A = -1; B = 0; C = 2 #Tribonacci
s = 0 #Sumatoria

for i in range(1, n+1, 1):
    flag = 1
    #Divisores serie fibonacci
    c = a + b
    a=b; b=c
    #print(c)

    #Serie tribonacci
    D = A + B + C
    A=B; B=C; C=D;
    #print(D)
    
    # exponente Serie primo
    while(flag == 1):
        if(num % d == 0):
            if(num == d):
                #Salida
                #Sumatoria
                if(i % 2 == 0):
                    #print("- ",D,x,"^",num,"/",c)
                    s = float(s - (D*math.pow((x),num))/c)
                else:
                    #print("+ ",D,x,"^",num,"/",c)
                    s = float(s + (D*math.pow((x),num))/c)
                flag = 0
            d = 2
            num = num + 1
        else:
            d = d + 1
s = round(s,2)
print(s)

#Sumatoria 2
#Entrada
import math
while True:
    try:
        n, x = map(int, input().split())
        while( 1 < n > 5 or 1 < x > 20):
            n, x = map(int, input().split())
            
        #Valores
        num = 2; d=2; flag = 1;#(Verdad) #n° Primos
        a = 1;b = 0 #fibonacci
        A = -1; B = 0; C = 2 #Tribonacci
        s = 0 #Sumatoria
        
        for i in range(1, n+1, 1):
            flag = 1
            #Divisores serie fibonacci
            c = a + b
            a=b; b=c
            #print(c)
        
            #Serie tribonacci
            D = A + B + C
            A=B; B=C; C=D;
            #print(D)
            
            # exponente Serie primo
            while(flag == 1):
                if(num % d == 0):
                    if(num == d):
                        #Salida
                        #Sumatoria
                        if(i % 2 == 0):
                            #print("- ",D,x,"^",num,"/",c)
                            s = float(s - (D*math.pow((x),num))/c)
                        else:
                            #print("+ ",D,x,"^",num,"/",c)
                            s = float(s + (D*math.pow((x),num))/c)
                        flag = 0
                    d = 2
                    num = num + 1
                else:
                    d = d + 1
        s = round(s,2)
        print("{0:.2f}".format(s))
    except EOFError:
        break

YoelTLaura:Problem1494:Compile Error
#Sumatoria1
#Entrada
import math
while True:
    try:
        n, x = map(int, input().split())
        while( 1 < n > 40 or 1 < x > 40):
            n, x = map(int, input().split())
        #Valores
        a=1; b=0                #fibonaci
        num=2; d=2              #n° Primo 
        s=0                     #Sumatoria

        #Proceso
        for i in range (1, n+1, 1):
            flag = 1 #(Verdad)
            #serie fibonacci
            c = a + b
            a=b; b=c
            
            # exponente Serie primo
            while(flag == 1):
                if(num % d == 0):
                    if(num == d):
                        #Sumatoria
                        s = float(s + (c/(num*x)))
                        flag = 0
                    d = 2
                    num = num + 1
                else:
                    d = d + 1
        #Salida
        print("{0:.2f}".format(s))
    except EOFError:
        break

            n, x = map(int, input().split())
        #Valores
        a=1; b=0
        num=2; d=2
        s=0
        #Proceso
        for i in range (1, n+1, 1):
            flag = 1 #(Verdad)
            #serie fibonacci
            c = a + b
            a=b; b=c    
            # exponente Serie primo
            while(flag == 1):
                if(num % d == 0):
                    if(num == d):
                        #Sumatoria
                        s = float(s + (c/(num*x)))
                        flag = 0
                    d = 2
                    num = num + 1
                else:
                    d = d + 1
        #Salida
        s = round(s,2)
        print(s)
    except EOFError:
        break

            while(flag == 1):

        n = int(input())
        while(0 > n > 10**3):
            n = int(input())

        num = 1 #número de puntos

                print(P)
            num = num + 3

for datos in sys.stdin:
    n= int(datos)
    sum = 0
    for c in range(1,n+1,1):
        if (c==n):
            sum = int((c*(3*(c)-1)/2))

import math
try:
    while True:
        n,x=map(int,input().split())
        while(n<1 or n>40 or x<1 or x>40):
            n,x=map(int,input().split())
        p=2
        r=0
        a=1
        b=0
        for i in range(1,n+1):
            if i%2==1:
                c=a+b
                a=b
                b=c
                r=r+(c/(p*x))
            else:
                c=a+b
                a=b
                b=c
                r=r+(c/(p*x))
            p+=1
            while True:
                sw=True
                ra=int(math.sqrt(p))+1
                for j in range(2,ra):
                    if(p%j==0):
                        sw=False
                if sw:
                    break
                p+=1
        print("{:.2f}".format(r))
except EOFError:

ariosl:Problem1495:Accepted
import math
while True:
    try:
        n, x = map(int, input().split())
        while( 1 < n > 5 or 1 < x > 20):
            n, x = map(int, input().split())
        num = 2; d=2; flag = 1;
        a = 1;b = 0 
        A = -1; B = 0; C = 2 
        s = 0 
        for i in range(1, n+1, 1):
            flag = 1
            c = a + b
            a=b; b=c
            D = A + B + C
            A=B; B=C; C=D;
            
            while(flag == 1):
                if(num % d == 0):
                    if(num == d):
                        if(i % 2 == 0):
                            s = float(s - (D*math.pow((x),num))/c)
                        else:
                            s = float(s + (D*math.pow((x),num))/c)
                        flag = 0
                    d = 2
                    num = num + 1
                else:
                    d = d + 1
        s = round(s,2)
        print("{0:.2f}".format(s))
    except EOFError:
        break

    try:
        n, m = map(int,input().split())
        prim = 2
        a = -1
        b = 0
        c = 2
        a1 = 1
        b1 = 0
        sw = True
        res = 0
        for i in range(0,m):
            d = a + b + c
            c1 = a1 + b1
            pow = n**prim
            par = (d * pow) / c1
        if sw:
            res = res + par
            sw = False
        else:
            res = res - par
            sw = True
        a = b
        b = c
        c = d
        a1 = b1
        b1 = c1
        while True:
            prim += 1
            cont = 0

n,x = map(int,input().split())

while (1<=n<=5 and 1<=x<=20):
    primo = 2; a = -1; w = 1
    j = 1; b = 0; y = 0
    k = 0; c = 2; suma = 0
    for i in range (1,n+1,1):
        while (j <= primo):
            if (primo%j == 0):
                k +=1
            j +=1
            if (k == 3):
                k = 0
                j = 1
                primo +=1
        k = 0
        j = 1

        e = a + b + c
        a = b
        b = c
        c = e

        z = w + y
        w = y
        y = z
    
        if (i%2 == 0):
            suma  = suma - (e*math.pow(x, primo)) / z
        else:
            suma  = suma + (e*math.pow(x, primo)) / z
        primo +=1

import math

try:
    while True:
        n,x = map(int,input().split())
        primo = 2; a = -1; w = 1
        j = 1; b = 0; y = 0
        k = 0; c = 2; suma = 0
        for i in range (1,n+1,1):
            while (j <= primo):
                if (primo%j == 0):
                    k +=1
                j +=1
                if (k == 3):
                    k = 0
                    j = 1
                    primo +=1
            k = 0
            j = 1

            e = a + b + c
            a = b
            b = c
            c = e

            z = w + y
            w = y
            y = z
    
            if (i%2 == 0):
                suma  = suma - (e*math.pow(x, primo)) / z
            else:
                suma  = suma + (e*math.pow(x, primo)) / z
            primo +=1

        suma = round(suma, 2)
        print(suma)
except EOFError:
    pass

alvaro_cs:Problem1495:Accepted
import math

try:
    while True:
        n,x = map(int,input().split())
        primo = 2; a = -1; w = 1
        j = 1; b = 0; y = 0
        k = 0; c = 2; suma = 0
        for i in range (1,n+1,1):
            while (j <= primo):
                if (primo%j == 0):
                    k +=1
                j +=1
                if (k == 3):
                    k = 0
                    j = 1
                    primo +=1
            k = 0
            j = 1

            e = a + b + c
            a = b
            b = c
            c = e

            z = w + y
            w = y
            y = z
    
            if (i%2 == 0):
                suma  = suma - (e*math.pow(x, primo)) / z
            else:
                suma  = suma + (e*math.pow(x, primo)) / z
            primo +=1

        print("{:.2f}".format(suma))
except EOFError:
    pass

WilliamDacio1:Problem1741:Time Limit Exceed
x = int(input())
while x < 0 or x >361:
    x = int(input())
i=0
pot = 3
s=0
try:
    while True:
        div = x ** pot
        fac=1
        divd=1
        while fac <= pot:
            divd = divd * fac
            fac = fac + 1
        pot = pot + 1
        if i%2==0:
            sig = 1
        else:
            sig = -1
        s = s + ((div/divd)*sig)
    print("{:.2f}".format(s))
    
except EOFError:
    pass

naquispe:Problem1494:Accepted
import math
try:
    while True:
        n,x=map(int,input().split())
        while(n<1 or n>40 or x<1 or x>40):
            n,x=map(int,input().split())
        p=2
        r=0
        a=1
        b=0
        for i in range(1,n+1):
            if i%2==1:
                c=a+b
                a=b
                b=c
                r=r+(c/(p*x))
            else:
                c=a+b
                a=b
                b=c
                r=r+(c/(p*x))
            p+=1
            while True:
                sw=True
                ra=int(math.sqrt(p))+1
                for j in range(2,ra):
                    if(p%j==0):
                        sw=False

import math
try:
    while True:
        n,x=map(int,input().split())
        while(n<1 or n>5 or x<1 or x>20):
            n,x=map(int,input().split())
        p=2
        r=0
        a=1
        b=0
        x1=-1
        y=0
        z=2
        for i in range(1,n+1):
            if i%2==1:
                c=a+b
                a=b
                b=c
                zr=x1+y+z
                x1=y
                y=z
                z=zr
                r=r+((zr*(x**p))/c)
            else:
                c=a+b
                a=b
                b=c
                zr=x1+y+z
                x1=y
                y=z
                z=zr
                r=r-((zr*(x**p))/c)
            p+=1
            while True:
                sw=True
                ra=int(math.sqrt(p))+1
                for j in range(2,ra):
                    if(p%j==0):
                        sw=False
                if sw:
                    break
                p+=1
        print("{:.2f}".format(r))
except EOFError:
    pass

ElizabethCusi11:Problem1494:Accepted
import math
while True:
	try:
		n,x = map(int,input().split())
		while(n<1 and n>40 and x<1 and x>40):
			n,x = map(int,input().split())
		a1=1
		b1=0
		c1=0
		p = 0  
		c = 3   
		r = 2
		d=r
		a=7
		z=0
		while p < n:
		  fact1 = math.factorial(c-1)
		  if fact1 % c == c-1:
		      c1=c1+a1
		      a1=b1
		      b1=c1 
		      z=(c1/(d*x))+z   
		      d=c
		      p += 1
		  c += 1
		print ("{:.2f}".format(z))	
	except EOFError:
	  break

sergiofn62:Problem1495:Accepted
# problema J sumatoria 2
while True:
    try:


        n,x = map(int,input().split())
        i = 1
        #fibonaci1
        a1 = -1
        b1 = 0
        c1 = 2
        # fibonaci 2
        a2 = 1
        b2 = 0
        #signo
        signo = 1
        suma = 0
        while i <= n:
            fibo1 = a1 + b1 + c1
            fibo2 = a2 + b2
            # fibo 1
            a1 = b1
            b1 = c1
            c1 = fibo1
            # fibo 2
            a2 = b2
            b2 = fibo2
            j = 1   #primo
            a = 2
            b = 2
            c = 1
            while j <= i:
                if a >= b:
                    if a % b == 0:
                        c = c + 1
                    b = b + 1
                else:
                    if c == 2:
                        primo = a
                        j = j + 1
                    a = a + 1
                    b = 2
                    c = 1

            suma = suma + signo * (fibo1 *x**primo)/fibo2
            i = i + 1
            signo = signo*-1
        print("{0:.2f}".format(suma))
    except EOFError:
        break

July50:Problem1495:Accepted
import math
try:
    while True:
        n,x=map(int,input().split())
        while(n<1 or n>5 or x<1 or x>20):
            n,x=map(int,input().split())
        m=2;t=0;e=1;f=0;j=-1;p=0;h=2;
        for q in range(1,n+1):
            if q%2==1:
                g=e+f;e=f;f=g;ht=j+p+h;j=p;p=h;h=ht;t=t+((ht*(x**m))/g);
            else:
                g=e+f;e=f;f=g;ht=j+p+h;j=p;p=h;h=ht;t=t-((ht*(x**m))/g);
            m=m+1
            while True:
                sw=True
                te=int(math.sqrt(m))+1
                for u in range(2,te):
                    if(m%u==0):
                        sw=False
                if sw:
                    break
                m=m+1
        print("{:.2f}".format(t))
except EOFError:
    pass

r = 1
t = 1
a = 0
z = 0
for j in range(y):
    x = int(input())
    if x > 3 :
        s = 0
        r = 1
        t = 1
        a = 0
        z = 0
        for i in range(x-3): 
            a = s + r + t
            z = z + a
            s = r
            r = t
            t = a
            i = i + 1
        z = z + 2
        print(z)
        z = 0
        
    elif x == 1:
        z = 0
        print(z)
    elif x == 2:
        z = 1
        print(z)
    elif x == 3:
        z = 2
        print(z)

cmedina:Problem1488:Runtime Error
# problema F sumatoria 1
try:
    while True:
        n,k = map(int,input().split())
        x = 1
        y = 0
        j = 1
        s = 0
        while j <= n:
            a = 2
            b = 2
            c = 1
            i = 1
            while i <= j:
                if a >= b:
                    if a % b == 0:
                        c = c + 1
                    b = b + 1
                else:
                    if c == 2:
                        primo = a
                        i = i + 1
                    a = a + 1
                    b = 2
                    c = 1
            fibo = x + y
            x = y
            y = fibo
            s = s + fibo/(primo*k)
            j = j + 1
        print("{0:.2f}".format(s))
except EOFError:
    pass

allaure:Problem1520:Compile Error
import math
def farey(n):
    a = [0,1]
    b = [1,n]
    nmax = math.factorial(n)
    for k in range(1, nmax):
        lam = math.floor((b[k-1] + n)/b[k])
        a.append(lam*a[k] - a[k-1])
        b.append(lam*b[k] - b[k-1])
        if (a[k+1] == 1) and (b[k+1] == 1):
            break
    return a, b
    
a,b = farey(3)
c = ["%d/%d" % t for t in zip(a,b)]

print(" ".join(c)

PyTHON3:Problem1494:Wrong Answer
#1,1,2,3,5
def fibo(num):
    """return the number at index `num` in the fibonacci sequence"""
    if num <= 2:
        return 1
    return fibo(num - 1) + fibo(num - 2)
#2,3,5,7,11
def prime(num):
    def si_esprimo(n):
        contador=0
        for i in range(1,n+1):
            if n%i==0:
                contador+=1
        if contador==2:
            return True
        else: return False            
    i=1
    a=2
    while i <=num:
        if si_esprimo(a):
            i+=1
            if i<=num:
                a+=1
        else:
            a+=1    
    return a        
n,x=map(int,input().split())
a=1
s=0
for j in range(n):
    s+=fibo(a)/(prime(a)*x)
    a+=1
print("{:0.2f}".format(s))

#1,1,2,3,5
def fibo(num):
    """return the number at index `num` in the fibonacci sequence"""
    if num <= 2:
        return 1
    return fibo(num - 1) + fibo(num - 2)
#2,3,5,7,11
def prime(num):
    def si_esprimo(n):
        contador=0
        for i in range(1,n+1):
            if n%i==0:
                contador+=1
        if contador==2:
            return True
        else: return False            
    i=1
    a=2
    while i <=num:
        if si_esprimo(a):
            i+=1
            if i<=num:
                a+=1
        else:
            a+=1    
    return a  
while 1:
    try:          
        n,x=map(int,input().split())
        a=1
        s=0
        for j in range(n):
            s+=fibo(a)/(prime(a)*x)
            a+=1
        print("{:0.2f}".format(s))   
    except:
        break

import sys
import math
for lin in sys.stdin:
    if(lin=="\n"):
        break
    n, x=map(int, lin.split())
    a=1
    b=0
    cont=1
    s=0
    serief=0
    cT=1
    bT=2
    aT=0
    serieT=1
    num=-1
    for i in range(0, n, 1):
        serief=a+b
        a=b
        b=serief
        while True:
            div=0
            cont=cont+1
            for j in range(1, int(cont/2)+1, 1):
                if(cont%j==0):
                    div=div+1
            if(div<2):
                break
        prim=cont
        s=s+(((serieT*math.pow(x, prim))/serief)*math.pow(num, i))
        serieT=cT+bT+aT
        aT=bT
        bT=cT
        cT=serieT
    print("{0:.2f}".format(s))

def si_esprimo(n):
        for i in range(2,n):
            if n%i==0:
                return False
        return True

for k in range(40):

        s=0
        for j in range(n):
            s+=fibo[c-1]/(prime[c-1]*x)
            c+=1
        print("{:0.2f}".format(s)) 
    except: break

PyTHON3:Problem1495:Accepted
tribo=[1,3,6,10,19]
fibo=[1,1,2,3,5]
prime=[2,3,5,7,11]
while 1:
    try:
        n,x=map(int,input().split())
        sw=True
        a=s=0
        for i in range(n):
            if sw:
                s+=(tribo[a]*pow(x,prime[a]))/fibo[a]
                a+=1
                sw=False
            else:
                s+=((tribo[a]*pow(x,prime[a]))/fibo[a])*-1
                a+=1
                sw=True    
        print("{:0.2f}".format(s))
    except: break

glorypatito:Problem1494:Time Limit Exceed
while True:
    try:
        n, x = map(int, input().split())
        s = 0
        d = 2
        p = 2
        a = 1
        b = 0
        c = 1
        aux = 1
        t = 1
        for i in range(1, n + 1, 1):
            f = a + b
            a = b
            b = f
            while c <= aux:
                if p % d == 0:
                    if p == d:
                        pi = x * p
                        s = s + f / pi
                        c = c + 1
                    d = 2
                    p = p + 1
                else:
                    d = d + 1
            aux = aux + 1
        s = round(s, 2)
        print(s)
    except EOFError:
        pass

        print("0.00")

       x=int(lin)*(math.pi/180)
       s=x

       d=6

    cont=0

    while f<=nu:
        if nu%f==0:
            cont+=1
            f+=1
            if cont>2:
                nu+=1
                f=1
                cont=0

            f+=1

        b=c

Latq:Problem1494:Accepted
import math
try:
    while True:
        n,x=map(int,input().split())
        i=1
        a=1
        b=1
        j=1
        suma=0
        while j<=n:
              d=math.factorial(i-1)+1
              if d%i==0 and i>1:
                j=j+1
                suma=suma+(a/(i*x))
                b=a+b
                a=b-a
              i=i+1
        print("{:.2f}".format(suma))
except EOFError:
    pass

Latq:Problem1495:Compile Error
import math
try:
    while True:
        n,x=map(int,input().split())
        if n==1:
            suma=x**2
            print("{:.2f}".format(suma))
        elif n==2:
            suma=(x**2)-(3*(x**3))
            print("{:.2f}".format(suma))
        elif n==3:
            suma=(x**2)-(3*(x**3))+(6*(x**5))/2
            print("{:.2f}".format(suma))
        elif n==4:
            suma=(x**2)-(3*(x**3))+((6*(x**5))/2)-((10*(x**7))/3)
            print("{:.2f}".format(suma))
        elif n==5:
            suma=(x**2)-(3*(x**3))+((6*(x**5))/2)-((10*(x**7))/3)+((19*(x**11))/5)
            print("{:.2f}".format(suma))
except EOFError:
    pass

    n , k = map (int,input().split())
    for i in range (0,n+1,1):
        s1 = s1 + i + k
        s2 = s2 + 2 + i + k
        div = (s1/s2)+ div
    print("{0:.0f}".format(div))
    div = 0
    s1 = 0
    s2 = 0
    if (n<=1 or n>=100 and k<=1 or k>=100):

for i in range(1,n+1):
    cont=0
    f=1
    t=t*(-1)
    while f<=nu:
        if nu%f==0:
            cont+=1
            f+=1
            if cont>2:
                nu+=1
                f=1
                cont=0
        else:
            f+=1
    if cont==2:
        c=a+b
        a=b
        b=c
        z=w+x+y
        w=x
        x=y
        y=z
        res=res+(t*((z*((l)**nu))/c))
        nu+=1
print("{:.2f}".format(res))

    while True:
        n, x = map(int, input().split())
        a = 1
        b = 0
        s = 0
        j = 2
        h = 2
        for i in range(n):
            div = a + b
            a = b
            b = div
            sw = 0
            while sw == 0:
                if j%h==0:
                    if j == h:
                        divi = j

carolinakantuta123:Problem1494:Accepted
try:
    while True:
        n,k = map(int,input().split())
        x = 1
        y = 0
        j = 1
        s = 0
        while j <= n:
            a = 2
            b = 2
            c = 1
            i = 1
            while i <= j:
                if a >= b:
                    if a % b == 0:
                        c = c + 1
                    b = b + 1
                else:
                    if c == 2:
                        primo = a
                        i = i + 1
                    a = a + 1
                    b = 2
                    c = 1
            fibo = x + y
            x = y
            y = fibo
            s = s + fibo/(primo*k)
            j = j + 1
        print("{0:.2f}".format(s))
except EOFError:

carolinakantuta123:Problem1495:Accepted
while True:
    try:
        n,x = map(int,input().split())
        i = 1
        #fibonaci1
        a1 = -1
        b1 = 0
        c1 = 2
        # fibonaci 2
        a2 = 1
        b2 = 0
        #signo
        signo = 1
        suma = 0
        while i <= n:
            fibo1 = a1 + b1 + c1
            fibo2 = a2 + b2
            # fibo 1
            a1 = b1
            b1 = c1
            c1 = fibo1
            # fibo 2
            a2 = b2
            b2 = fibo2
            j = 1   #primo
            a = 2
            b = 2
            c = 1
            while j <= i:
                if a >= b:
                    if a % b == 0:
                        c = c + 1
                    b = b + 1
                else:
                    if c == 2:
                        primo = a
                        j = j + 1
                    a = a + 1
                    b = 2
                    c = 1

            suma = suma + signo * (fibo1 *x**primo)/fibo2
            i = i + 1
            signo = signo*-1
        print("{0:.2f}".format(suma))
    except EOFError:
        break

    while True:
        n, x = map(int, input().split())
        s = 0
        d = 2
        p = 2
        a = 1
        b = 0
        c = 1
        aux = 1
        t = 1
        for i in range(1, n + 1, 1):
            f = a + b
            a = b
            b = f
            while c <= aux:
                if p % d == 0:
                    if p == d:
                        pi = x * p
                        s = s + f / pi
                        c = c + 1
                    d = 2
                    p = p + 1
                else:
                    d = d + 1

mnguerrero:Problem1495:Accepted
import math
while True:
    try:
        n, x = map(int, input().split())
        while( 1 < n > 5 or 1 < x > 20):
            n, x = map(int, input().split())
            
        
        num = 2; d=2; flag = 1;#(Verdad) #n° Primos
        a = 1;b = 0 #fibonacci
        A = -1; B = 0; C = 2 #Tribonacci
        s = 0 #Sumatoria
        
        for i in range(1, n+1, 1):
            flag = 1
            
            c = a + b
            a=b; b=c
            #print(c)
        
           
            D = A + B + C
            A=B; B=C; C=D;
            #print(D)
            
            
            while(flag == 1):
                if(num % d == 0):
                    if(num == d):
                        #Salida
                        #Sumatoria
                        if(i % 2 == 0):
                            #print("- ",D,x,"^",num,"/",c)
                            s = float(s - (D*math.pow((x),num))/c)
                        else:
                            #print("+ ",D,x,"^",num,"/",c)
                            s = float(s + (D*math.pow((x),num))/c)
                        flag = 0
                    d = 2
                    num = num + 1
                else:
                    d = d + 1
        s = round(s,2)
        print("{0:.2f}".format(s))
    except EOFError:
        break

daniSebas4:Problem1741:Accepted
#Daniel Sebastian Puña Saravia
import sys
import math
#Entrada/proceso/salida
for lin in sys.stdin:
    if(lin=="\n"):
        break
    else:
       x=int(lin)*(math.pi/180)
       if(x*(180/math.pi)==360):
           print("-0.00")
       else:
            s=x
            a=4
            d=6
            exp=3
            c=-1
            for i in range(1, 50, 1):
                s=s+(((math.pow(x,exp))/d)*math.pow(c, i))
                exp=exp+2
                d=d*a*(a+1)
                a=a+2
            print("{0:.2f}".format(s))

JhersonJMC:Problem1495:Accepted
while True:
    try:
        n, x = map(int, input().split())
        a = 1
        b = 0
        f = 0
        c = 1
        p = 2
        d = 2
        cont = 1
        s = 0
        q = 3
        w = -1
        z = 0
        d2 = q + w + z
        for i in range(1, n + 1, 1):
            q = w
            w = z
            z = d2
            d2 = q + w + z
            f = a + b
            a = b
            b = f
            while (c <= cont):
                if (p % d == 0):
                    if (p == d):
                        c = c + 1
                    d = 2
                    p = p + 1
                else:
                    d = d + 1

            p = p - 1

            if (i % 2 == 1):
                s = s + (d2 * (x ** p) / f)
            else:
                s = s - (d2 * (x ** p) / f)

            p = p + 1
            cont = cont + 1
        print("{:.2f}".format(round(s, 2)))
    except EOFError:
        break

9909074:Problem1495:Accepted
while True:
    try:
        n,x = map(int,input().split())
        i = 1
        #fibonaci1
        a1 = -1
        b1 = 0
        c1 = 2
        # fibonaci 2
        a2 = 1
        b2 = 0
        #signo
        signo = 1
        suma = 0
        while i <= n:
            fibo1 = a1 + b1 + c1
            fibo2 = a2 + b2
            # fibo 1
            a1 = b1
            b1 = c1
            c1 = fibo1
            # fibo 2
            a2 = b2
            b2 = fibo2
            j = 1 #primo
            a = 2
            b = 2
            c = 1
            while j <= i:
                if a >= b:
                    if a % b == 0:
                        c = c + 1
                    b = b + 1
                else:
                    if c == 2:
                        primo = a
                        j = j + 1
                    a = a + 1
                    b = 2
                    c = 1

            suma = suma + signo * (fibo1 *x**primo)/fibo2
            i = i + 1
            signo = signo*-1
        print("{0:.2f}".format(suma))
    except EOFError:
        break

            while sw == 0:
                if p%d==0:
                    if p == d :
                        expo = d
                        sw = 1
                    d = 2
                    p = p + 1
                else:
                    d = d+1
            divi = a + b
            a = b
            b = divi
            div= y + r + t
            y = r
            r = t
            t = div
            if i%2==0:
                sig = 1
            else:
                sig = -1
            s = s + (((div * (x**expo))/ divi)* sig)
        print("{:.2f}".format(s))

except:
    pass

    d=2

    h=1
    a1=1
    b1=0
    c1=0
    s=0
    div=0
    s2 = 0
    a2 = -1
    b2 = 2
    c2 = 0
    while c<n+1:
        if(p%d==0):
            if(p==d):
                if(m!=10):
                    if (c % 2 == 0):
                        if (h == 1):
                            h = 0
                        c1 = a1 + b1
                        a1 = b1
                        b1 = c1
                        s2 = a2 + b2 + c2
                        if (c == 3):
                            s2 = s2 + 2
                        elev = pow(x, p)
                        a2 = b2
                        b2 = c2
                        c2 = s2
                        p1 = s2 * elev
                        div = p1 / c1
                        s = s - div
                        c = c + 1
                        m = m + 1
                    else:
                        if (h == 1):
                            h = 0
                        c1 = a1 + b1
                        a1 = b1
                        b1 = c1
                        s2 = a2 + b2 + c2
                        if (c == 3):
                            s2 = s2 + 2
                        elev = pow(x, p)
                        a2 = b2
                        b2 = c2
                        c2 = s2
                        p1 = s2 * elev
                        div = p1 / c1
                        s = s + div
                        c = c + 1
                        m = m + 1

            d=2
            p=p+1
        else:
            d=d+1
    print("{:.2f}".format(s))

for linea in sys.stdin:
    if linea == "\n":
        break
    n, k = map(int, linea.split())
    s = 0
# PROCESO Y SALIDA

        s = s + a

9255156:Problem1495:Accepted
while True:
    try:
        n, l=map(int, input().split())
        if 1<=n<=5 and 1<=l<=20:
            nu=2
            a=1
            b=0
            c=0
            w=-1
            x=0
            y=2
            res=0
            t=-1
            for i in range(1,n+1):
                cont=0
                f=1
                t=t*(-1)
                while f<=nu:
                    if nu%f==0:
                        cont+=1
                        f+=1
                        if cont>2:
                            nu+=1
                            f=1
                            cont=0
                    else:
                        f+=1
                if cont==2:
                    c=a+b
                    a=b
                    b=c
                    z=w+x+y
                    w=x
                    x=y
                    y=z
                    res=res+(t*((z*((l)**nu))/c))
                    nu+=1
            print("{:.2f}".format(res))
    except EOFError:
        break

        n,x = map(int,input().split())

        #fibonaci1

        b1 = 0
        c1 = 2
        # fibonaci 2
        a2 = 1
        b2 = 0
        #signo
        signo = 1
        suma = 0
        while i <= n:
            fibo1 = a1 + b1 + c1
            fibo2 = a2 + b2
            # fibo 1
            a1 = b1
            b1 = c1
            c1 = fibo1
            # fibo 2
            a2 = b2
            b2 = fibo2
            j = 1   #primo
            a = 2
            b = 2
            c = 1
            while j <= i:
                if a >= b:
                    if a % b == 0:
                        c = c + 1
                    b = b + 1
                else:
                    if c == 2:
                        primo = a
                        j = j + 1
                    a = a + 1
                    b = 2
                    c = 1

9255156:Problem1494:Accepted
while True:
    try:
        n, x=map(int, input().split())
        f=2
        a=1
        resp=0
        b=0
        for i in range(1,n+1):
            cont=0
            j=1
            while j<=f:
                if f%j==0:
                    cont+=1
                    j+=1
                    if cont>2:
                        f+=1
                        cont=0
                        j=1
                else: j+=1
            if cont==2:
                c=a+b
                a=b
                b=c
                resp=(c/(f*x))+resp
                f+=1
        print("{:.2f}".format(resp))
    except EOFError:
        break

            a = 2
            b = 2
            c = 1

                if a >= b:

                        c = c + 1
                    b = b + 1

                        i = i + 1

                    c = 1

        n,x = map(int,input().split())
        i = 1
        #fibonaci1
        a1 = -1
        b1 = 0
        c1 = 2
        # fibonaci 2
        a2 = 1
        b2 = 0
        #signo
        signo = 1
        suma = 0
        while i <= n:
            fibo1 = a1 + b1 + c1
            fibo2 = a2 + b2
            # fibo 1
            a1 = b1
            b1 = c1
            c1 = fibo1
            # fibo 2
            a2 = b2
            b2 = fibo2
            j = 1   #primo
            a = 2
            b = 2
            c = 1

                if a >= b:

                        c = c + 1
                    b = b + 1

                        j = j + 1

Alevelma:Problem1494:Accepted
import math
try:
    while True:
        n,x=map(int,input().split())
        while(n<1 or n>40 or x<1 or x>40):
            n,x=map(int,input().split())
        p=2
        r=0
        a=1
        b=0
        for i in range(1,n+1):
            if i%2==1:
                c=a+b
                a=b
                b=c
                r=r+(c/(p*x))
            else:
                c=a+b
                a=b
                b=c
                r=r+(c/(p*x))
            p+=1
            while True:
                sw=True
                ra=int(math.sqrt(p))+1
                for j in range(2,ra):
                    if(p%j==0):
                        sw=False
                if sw:
                    break
                p+=1
        print("{:.2f}".format(r))
except EOFError:
    pass

while True:
    try:
        n, x = map(int, input().split())
        s = 0
        d = 2
        p = 2
        a = 1
        b = 0
        c = 1
        aux = 1
        t = 1
        for i in range(1, n + 1, 1):
            f = a + b
            a = b
            b = f
            while c <= aux:
                if p % d == 0:
                    if p == d:
                        pi = x * p
                        s = s + f / pi
                        c = c + 1
                    d = 2
                    p = p + 1
                else:
                    d = d + 1
            aux = aux + 1
        print("{0:.2f}".format(s))

            a = 2
            b = 2
            c = 1
            i = 1
            while i <= m:
                if a >= b:
                    if a % b == 0:
                        c = c +1
                    b = b + 1
                else:
                    if c == 2:
                        primo = a
                        i = i + 1
                    a = a + 1
                    b = 2
                    c = 1
            fibo = x + y
            x = y
            y = fibo
            l = l + fibo/(primo*k)
            m = m + 1
        print("{0:.2f}".format(l))
except EOFError:
    pass

while True:
    try:
        n,x = map(int,input().split())
        i = 1
        #fibonaci1
        a1 = -1
        b1 = 0
        c1 = 2
        # fibonaci 2
        a2 = 1
        b2 = 0
        #signo
        signo = 1
        suma = 0
        while i <= n:
            fibo1 = a1 + b1 + c1
            fibo2 = a2 + b2
            # fibo 1
            a1 = b1
            b1 = c1
            c1 = fibo1
            # fibo 2
            a2 = b2
            b2 = fibo2
            j = 1   #primo
            a = 2
            b = 2
            c = 1
            while j <= i:
                if a >= b:
                    if a % b == 0:
                        c = c + 1
                    b = b + 1
                else:
                    if c == 2:
                        primo = a
                        j = j + 1
                    a = a + 1
                    b = 2
                    c = 1

            suma = suma + signo * (fibo1 *x**primo)/fibo2
            i = i + 1
            signo = signo*-1
        print("{0:.2f}".format(suma))
    except EOFError:

EVA_BAUTISTA:Problem1494:Accepted
try:
    while True:
        n,k = map(int,input().split())
        x = 1
        y = 0
        m = 1
        l = 0
        while m <= n:
            a = 2
            b = 2
            c = 1
            i = 1
            while i <= m:
                if a >= b:
                    if a % b == 0:
                        c = c +1
                    b = b + 1
                else:
                    if c == 2:
                        primo = a
                        i = i + 1
                    a = a + 1
                    b = 2
                    c = 1
            fibo = x + y
            x = y
            y = fibo
            l = l + fibo/(primo*k)
            m = m + 1
        print("{0:.2f}".format(l))
except EOFError:
    pass

    try: 
        n,x = map(int,input().split()) 
        i = 1 
        #fibonaci1 
        a1 = -1 
        b1 = 0 
        c1 = 2 
        # fibonaci 2 
        a2 = 1 
        b2 = 0 
        #signo 
        signo = 1 
        suma = 0 
        while i <= n: 
            fibo1 = a1 + b1 + c1 
            fibo2 = a2 + b2 
            # fibo 1 
            a1 = b1 
            b1 = c1 
            c1 = fibo1 
            # fibo 2 
            a2 = b2 
            b2 = fibo2 
            j = 1   #primo 
            a = 2 
            b = 2 
            c = 1 
            while j <= i: 
                if a >= b: 
                    if a % b == 0: 
                        c = c + 1 
                    b = b + 1 
                else: 
                    if c == 2: 
                        primo = a 
                        j = j + 1

                    c = 1

    t=int(input())

    while i<1 or i>n:
        i=int(input())
        
    xi.append(i)
    

    a=a+1

fi=[]
a=0


while a<t:
    j=int(input())

    while j<1 or j>n:
        j=int(input())
        
    fi.append(j)
    

    a=a+1

resultado=list(map(lambda x,y: x*y, xi, fi))

def sumar(resultado):

    if resultado==[]:
        suma=0

    else:
        suma= resultado[0] + sumar(resultado[1:])

    return suma

media = sumar(resultado) / n

print("\n")
